Parsing script:
async def parse_clothing_sections(html: str):
    soup = BeautifulSoup(html, 'html.parser')
    clothing_sections = []
    meta_tags = soup.find_all('meta', {'name': 'description'})
    for tag in meta_tags:
        if 'dresses' in tag.get('content', '').lower():
            clothing_sections.append(tag['content'])
    og_tags = soup.find_all('meta', {'property': 'og:description'})
    for tag in og_tags:
        if 'dresses' in tag.get('content', '').lower():
            clothing_sections.append(tag['content'])
    twitter_tags = soup.find_all('meta', {'name': 'twitter:description'})
    for tag in twitter_tags:
        if 'dresses' in tag.get('content', '').lower():
            clothing_sections.append(tag['content'])
    return clothing_sections

Parsing script:
async def parse_clothing_sections(html: str):
    soup = BeautifulSoup(html, 'html.parser')
    clothing_sections = []
    clothing_keywords = ['product', 'collection', 'grid-product', 'product-single', 'product__photos', 'product__thumbs']
    for section in soup.find_all(True, {'class': True}):
        class_list = section.get('class')
        if any((keyword in class_list for keyword in clothing_keywords)):
            clothing_sections.append(str(section))
    return clothing_sections

async def parse_clothing_sections(html: str):
    soup = BeautifulSoup(html, 'html.parser')
    clothing_sections = []
    for section in soup.find_all(class_='grid-product'):
        clothing_sections.append(str(section))

Parsing script:
async def parse_clothing_sections(html: str):
    soup = BeautifulSoup(html, 'html.parser')
    script_tag = soup.find('script', {'data-campaign': True})
    if not script_tag:
        return []
    script_content = script_tag.string.strip()
    start_index = script_content.find('{')
    end_index = script_content.rfind('}')
    if start_index == -1 or end_index == -1:
        return []
    json_str = script_content[start_index:end_index + 1]
    try:
        data = json.loads(json_str)
    except json.JSONDecodeError:
        return []
    clothing_sections = []
    collection = data.get('collection', {})
    products = collection.get('products', [])
    for product in products:
        clothing_sections.append({'id': product.get('id'), 'price': product.get('price'), 'title': product.get('title'), 'variant': product.get('variant'), 'compare_price': product.get('compare_price'), 'collections': product.get('collections')})
    return clothing_sections

Parsing script:
async def parse_clothing_sections(html: str):
    soup = BeautifulSoup(html, 'html.parser')
    script_tags = soup.find_all('script')
    clothing_sections = []
    for script in script_tags:
        try:
            data = json.loads(script.string)
            if isinstance(data, list):
                for item in data:
                    if 'title' in item and 'price' in item:
                        clothing_sections.append(item)
        except (json.JSONDecodeError, TypeError):
            continue
    return clothing_sections

Parsing script:
async def parse_clothing_sections(html: str):
    soup = BeautifulSoup(html, 'html.parser')
    script_tags = soup.find_all('script')
    clothing_data = []
    for script in script_tags:
        if script.string and 'variant' in script.string:
            try:
                json_data = script.string.strip()
                start_index = json_data.find('[')
                end_index = json_data.rfind(']')
                if start_index != -1 and end_index != -1:
                    json_data = json_data[start_index:end_index + 1]
                    clothing_items = json.loads(json_data)
                    clothing_data.extend(clothing_items)
            except json.JSONDecodeError:
                continue
    return clothing_data

Parsing script:
async def parse_clothing_sections(html: str):
    soup = BeautifulSoup(html, 'html.parser')
    clothing_sections = []
    clothing_keywords = ['product', 'collection', 'variant', 'swatch', 'price', 'size']
    for section in soup.find_all():
        section_text = section.get_text().lower()
        if any((keyword in section_text for keyword in clothing_keywords)):
            clothing_sections.append(section)
    return clothing_sections

Parsing script:
async def parse_clothing_sections(html: str):
    soup = BeautifulSoup(html, 'html.parser')
    clothing_sections = []
    clothing_selectors = ['.product-index', '.product-list-item', '.product--root', '.product-thumbnail', '.collection-page__product', '[data-product-item]', '[data-product-grid-item]', '[data-product-grid]', '.product-card', '.product-details', '.product-price', '.product-item__price']
    for selector in clothing_selectors:
        elements = soup.select(selector)
        for element in elements:
            clothing_sections.append(str(element))
    return clothing_sections

Parsing script:
async def parse_clothing_sections(html: str):
    soup = BeautifulSoup(html, 'html.parser')
    clothing_sections = []
    clothing_selectors = ['.product-item', '.product-block', '.grid-view-item', '.product-grid-item', '.product-card', '.product-index', '.product-list-item', '.product--root', '.product-thumbnail', '.collection-page__product', '[data-product-item]', '[data-product-grid-item]', '[data-product-grid]']
    for selector in clothing_selectors:
        elements = soup.select(selector)
        for element in elements:
            clothing_sections.append(str(element))
    return clothing_sections

Parsing script:
async def parse_clothing_sections(html: str):
    soup = BeautifulSoup(html, 'html.parser')
    clothing_sections = []
    clothing_keywords = ['product', 'variant', 'swatch', 'price', 'size', 'collection']
    for section in soup.find_all():
        if any((keyword in section.get('class', []) for keyword in clothing_keywords)):
            clothing_sections.append(str(section))
    return clothing_sections

async def parse_clothing_sections(html: str):
    soup = BeautifulSoup(html, 'html.parser')
    clothing_sections = []
    clothing_selectors = ['[class*="product"]', '[class*="collection"]', '[class*="grid"]', '[class*="item"]', '[class*="card"]', '[class*="price"]', '[class*="title"]', '[class*="heading"]', '[class*="variant"]', '[class*="option"]', '[class*="swatch"]', '[class*="image"]', '[class*="media"]', '[class*="thumbnail"]', '[class*="details"]', '[class*="caption"]', '[class*="info"]', '[class*="meta"]', '[class*="details"]', '[class*="caption"]', '[class*="info"]', '[class*="meta"]']
    for selector in clothing_selectors:
        elements = soup.select(selector)
        for element in elements:
            clothing_sections.append(str(element))
    return clothing_sections

async def parse_clothing_sections(html: str):
    soup = BeautifulSoup(html, 'html.parser')
    clothing_sections = []
    selectors = ['.product-item', '.product-block', '.grid-view-item', '.product-grid li.grid__item', '.grid-product', '.product-grid-item', '.type-product-grid-item', '.product-card', '.product-index', '.product-list-item', '.product--root', '.product-thumbnail', '.collection-page__product', '[data-product-item]', '[data-product-grid-item]', '[data-product-grid]']
    for selector in selectors:
        sections = soup.select(selector)
        for section in sections:
            clothing_sections.append(str(section))
    return clothing_sections

Parsing script:
async def parse_clothing_sections(html: str):
    soup = BeautifulSoup(html, 'html.parser')
    clothing_sections = []
    clothing_keywords = ['product', 'collection', 'grid', 'item', 'card', 'price', 'variant', 'swatch']
    for div in soup.find_all(['div', 'section']):
        if any((keyword in div.get('class', []) for keyword in clothing_keywords)):
            clothing_sections.append(str(div))
    return clothing_sections

Parsing script:
async def parse_clothing_sections(html: str):
    soup = BeautifulSoup(html, 'html.parser')
    clothing_sections = []
    selectors = ['[data-section-type="product"]', '[data-section-type="featured-product"]', '[data-product-type="featured"]', '[data-section-type="product-template"]', '.product-item', '.product-block', '.grid-product', '.product-card', '.product-index', '.product-list-item', '.product-thumbnail', '[data-product-item]', '[data-product-grid-item]', '[data-product-grid]']
    for selector in selectors:
        sections = soup.select(selector)
        for section in sections:
            clothing_sections.append(str(section))
    return clothing_sections

Parsing script:
async def parse_clothing_sections(html: str):
    soup = BeautifulSoup(html, 'html.parser')
    clothing_sections = []
    clothing_keywords = ['shirt', 'pants', 'dress', 'jacket', 'clothing', 'apparel', 'fashion', 'wear']
    sections = soup.find_all('section')
    for section in sections:
        section_text = section.get_text().lower()
        section_classes = ' '.join(section.get('class', [])).lower()
        if any((keyword in section_text for keyword in clothing_keywords)) or any((keyword in section_classes for keyword in clothing_keywords)):
            clothing_sections.append(section)
    return clothing_sections

async def parse_clothing_sections(html: str):
    soup = BeautifulSoup(html, 'html.parser')
    clothing_sections = []
    clothing_keywords = ['product', 'collection', 'grid', 'item', 'card', 'thumbnail']
    for keyword in clothing_keywords:
        sections = soup.find_all(class_=lambda x: x and keyword in x)
        clothing_sections.extend(sections)
    return clothing_sections

Parsing script:
async def parse_clothing_sections(html: str):
    soup = BeautifulSoup(html, 'html.parser')
    clothing_sections = []
    clothing_keywords = ['shirt', 'pants', 'dress', 'skirt', 'jacket', 'coat', 'sweater', 'jeans', 'trousers', 'blouse', 't-shirt', 'shorts']
    for keyword in clothing_keywords:
        sections = soup.find_all(class_=lambda x: x and keyword in x.lower())
        clothing_sections.extend(sections)
    return clothing_sections

Parsing script:
async def parse_clothing_sections(html: str):
    soup = BeautifulSoup(html, 'html.parser')
    clothing_sections = []
    clothing_selectors = ['.ProductItem', '.product-item', '.product-block', '.grid-view-item', '.product-grid li.grid__item', '.grid-product', '.product-grid-item', '.type-product-grid-item', '.product-card', '.product-index', '.grid .card:not(.grid__item .card)', '.grid product-card', '.product-list-item', '.product--root', '.product-thumbnail', '.collection-page__product', '[data-product-item]', '[data-product-grid-item]', '[data-product-grid]']
    for selector in clothing_selectors:
        sections = soup.select(selector)
        for section in sections:
            clothing_sections.append(str(section))
    return clothing_sections

Parsing script:
async def parse_clothing_sections(html: str):
    soup = BeautifulSoup(html, 'html.parser')
    clothing_sections = []
    for section in soup.find_all(class_=['product-card__title', 'product-card__labels', 'collection__grid-item']):

    return clothing_sections

Parsing script:
async def parse_clothing_sections(html: str):
    soup = BeautifulSoup(html, 'html.parser')
    clothing_sections = []
    selectors = ['.ProductItem', '.product-item', '.product-block', '.grid-view-item', '.product-grid li.grid__item', '.grid-product', '.product-grid-item', '.type-product-grid-item', '.product-card', '.product-index', '.grid .card:not(.grid__item .card)', '.grid product-card', '.product-list-item', '.product--root', '.product-thumbnail', '.collection-page__product', '[data-product-item]', '[data-product-grid-item]', '[data-product-grid]']
    for selector in selectors:
        sections = soup.select(selector)
        for section in sections:
            clothing_sections.append(str(section))
    return clothing_sections

Parsing script:
async def parse_clothing_sections(html: str):
    soup = BeautifulSoup(html, 'html.parser')
    clothing_sections = []
    clothing_keywords = ['product', 'variant', 'swatch', 'price', 'size', 'collection']
    for section in soup.find_all(True):
        section_text = section.get_text().lower()
        if any((keyword in section_text for keyword in clothing_keywords)):
            clothing_sections.append(section)
    return clothing_sections

Parsing script:
async def parse_clothing_sections(html: str):
    soup = BeautifulSoup(html, 'html.parser')
    clothing_sections = []
    clothing_selectors = ['.product-index', '.product-list-item', '.product--root', '.product-thumbnail', '.collection-page__product', '[data-product-item]', '[data-product-grid-item]', '[data-product-grid]', '.product-details', '.product-price', '.product-card__price', '.product__price', '.product-item__price', '.product-list-item-price', '.product-item-price', '.product-card', '.product-grid-item', '.product-grid', '.product-item', '.product-block', '.grid-view-item', '.grid-product', '.type-product-grid-item']
    for selector in clothing_selectors:
        elements = soup.select(selector)
        for element in elements:
            clothing_sections.append(str(element))
    return clothing_sections

Parsing script:
async def parse_clothing_sections(html: str):
    soup = BeautifulSoup(html, 'html.parser')
    clothing_sections = []
    clothing_keywords = ['product', 'variant', 'swatch', 'price', 'collection']
    for section in soup.find_all():
        if any((keyword in section.get('class', []) for keyword in clothing_keywords)):
            clothing_sections.append(str(section))
    return clothing_sections

Parsing script:
async def parse_clothing_sections(html: str):
    soup = BeautifulSoup(html, 'html.parser')
    clothing_sections = []
    selectors = ['.product-item-price', '.product-item', '.product-block', '.grid-product', '.product-card', '.product-list-item', '.product-thumbnail', '[data-product-item]', '[data-product-grid-item]', '[data-product-grid]']
    for selector in selectors:
        sections = soup.select(selector)
        for section in sections:
            clothing_sections.append(str(section))
    return clothing_sections

Parsing script:
async def parse_clothing_sections(html: str):
    soup = BeautifulSoup(html, 'html.parser')
    clothing_sections = []
    clothing_related_classes = ['product-block', 'grid-product__content', 'grid-product__tag--sale', 'grid-product__tag--sold-out']
    for class_name in clothing_related_classes:
        sections = soup.find_all(class_=class_name)
        for section in sections:
            clothing_sections.append(str(section))
    return clothing_sections

Parsing script:
async def parse_clothing_sections(html: str):
    soup = BeautifulSoup(html, 'html.parser')
    clothing_sections = []
    clothing_related_classes = ['grid-product__tag--sale', 'grid-product__tag--sold-out', 'grid-product__price--original', 'grid-product__title', 'grid-product__image', 'grid-product__colors']
    for class_name in clothing_related_classes:
        sections = soup.find_all(class_=class_name)
        for section in sections:
            clothing_sections.append(str(section))
    return clothing_sections

Parsing script:
async def parse_clothing_sections(html: str):
    soup = BeautifulSoup(html, 'html.parser')
    script_tag = soup.find('script', text=lambda t: 'product_options' in t)
    if not script_tag:
        return None
    json_data = script_tag.string.strip()
    try:
        data = json.loads(json_data)
    except json.JSONDecodeError:
        return None
    clothing_sections = []
    product_options = data.get('product_options', [])
    for option in product_options:
        if option.get('name').lower() in ['size', 'style', 'color', 'sizes']:
            clothing_sections.append(option)
    return clothing_sections

Parsing script:
async def parse_clothing_sections(html: str):
    soup = BeautifulSoup(html, 'html.parser')
    script_tag = soup.find('script', id='bss-pl-config-data')
    if not script_tag:
        return []
    try:
        js_content = script_tag.string.strip()
        start_index = js_content.find('[')
        end_index = js_content.rfind(']') + 1
        json_data = js_content[start_index:end_index]
        config_data = json.loads(json_data)
        clothing_sections = []
        for item in config_data:
            if 'productType' in item and item['productType'] == 3:
                clothing_sections.append(item)
        return clothing_sections
    except Exception as e:
        print(f'Error parsing JSON: {e}')
        return []

async def parse_clothing_sections(html: str):
    soup = BeautifulSoup(html, 'html.parser')
    clothing_sections = []
    for section in soup.find_all('section'):
        if 'clothing' in section.get('class', []) or 'dress' in section.get_text().lower():

    return clothing_sections

Parsing script:
async def parse_clothing_sections(html: str):
    soup = BeautifulSoup(html, 'html.parser')
    clothing_sections = []
    try:
        json_data = json.loads(html)
        for item in json_data:
            product_info = {'title': item['product']['title'], 'vendor': item['product']['vendor'], 'price': item['price']['amount'], 'currency': item['price']['currencyCode'], 'url': item['product']['url'], 'image_src': item['image']['src'], 'sku': item['sku'], 'size': item['title']}
            clothing_sections.append(product_info)
    except json.JSONDecodeError:
        print('Error decoding JSON from HTML')
    return clothing_sections

Parsing script:
async def parse_clothing_sections(html: str):
    soup = BeautifulSoup(html, 'html.parser')
    script_tags = soup.find_all('script')
    clothing_sections = []
    for script in script_tags:
        if 'Floral' in script.text or 'Dress' in script.text:
            try:
                json_data = script.string.split(');', 1)[0].split('(', 1)[1]
                data = json.loads(json_data)
                if isinstance(data, list):
                    for item in data:
                        if 'product' in item:
                            clothing_sections.append(item)
            except (json.JSONDecodeError, IndexError):
                continue
    return clothing_sections

Parsing script:
async def parse_clothing_sections(html: str):
    soup = BeautifulSoup(html, 'html.parser')
    script_tag = soup.find('script', text=lambda t: 'var meta =' in t)
    if not script_tag:
        return []
    script_content = script_tag.string
    json_str = script_content.split('var meta =', 1)[1].strip().rstrip(';')
    try:
        meta_data = json.loads(json_str)
    except json.JSONDecodeError:
        return []
    clothing_sections = []
    for product in meta_data.get('products', []):
        product_info = {'id': product.get('id'), 'vendor': product.get('vendor'), 'type': product.get('type'), 'variants': []}
        for variant in product.get('variants', []):
            variant_info = {'id': variant.get('id'), 'price': variant.get('price'), 'name': variant.get('name'), 'public_title': variant.get('public_title'), 'sku': variant.get('sku')}
            product_info['variants'].append(variant_info)
        clothing_sections.append(product_info)
    return clothing_sections

Parsing script:
async def parse_clothing_sections(html: str):
    soup = BeautifulSoup(html, 'html.parser')
    try:
        data = json.loads(soup.text)
    except json.JSONDecodeError:
        return []
    clothing_sections = []
    for product in data:
        product_info = {'id': product.get('id'), 'vendor': product.get('vendor'), 'type': product.get('type'), 'variants': []}
        for variant in product.get('variants', []):
            variant_info = {'id': variant.get('id'), 'price': variant.get('price'), 'name': variant.get('name'), 'public_title': variant.get('public_title'), 'sku': variant.get('sku')}
            product_info['variants'].append(variant_info)
        clothing_sections.append(product_info)
    return clothing_sections

Parsing script:
async def parse_clothing_sections(html: str):
    soup = BeautifulSoup(html, 'html.parser')
    products = []
    for product_section in soup.find_all(text=True):
        if 'vendor' in product_section and 'variants' in product_section:
            products.append(product_section.strip())
    return products

Parsing script:
async def parse_clothing_sections(html: str):
    soup = BeautifulSoup(html, 'html.parser')
    json_data = html.strip()
    try:
        data = json.loads(json_data)
    except json.JSONDecodeError:
        return []
    clothing_sections = []
    for product in data:
        product_info = {'id': product.get('id'), 'gid': product.get('gid'), 'vendor': product.get('vendor'), 'type': product.get('type'), 'variants': []}
        for variant in product.get('variants', []):
            variant_info = {'id': variant.get('id'), 'price': variant.get('price'), 'name': variant.get('name'), 'public_title': variant.get('public_title'), 'sku': variant.get('sku')}
            product_info['variants'].append(variant_info)
        clothing_sections.append(product_info)
    return clothing_sections

async def parse_clothing_sections(html: str):
    soup = BeautifulSoup(html, 'html.parser')
    try:
        data = json.loads(html)
    except json.JSONDecodeError:
        return []
    clothing_sections = []
    for product in data:
        product_info = {'id': product.get('id'), 'gid': product.get('gid'), 'vendor': product.get('vendor'), 'type': product.get('type'), 'variants': []}
        for variant in product.get('variants', []):
            variant_info = {'id': variant.get('id'), 'price': variant.get('price'), 'name': variant.get('name'), 'public_title': variant.get('public_title'), 'sku': variant.get('sku')}
            product_info['variants'].append(variant_info)
        clothing_sections.append(product_info)
    return clothing_sections

Parsing script:
async def parse_clothing_sections(html: str):
    soup = BeautifulSoup(html, 'html.parser')
    script_tag = soup.find('script', type='application/ld+json')
    if not script_tag:
        return []
    try:
        data = json.loads(script_tag.string)
    except json.JSONDecodeError:
        return []
    clothing_sections = []
    for product in data.get('products', []):
        product_info = {'id': product.get('id'), 'vendor': product.get('vendor'), 'type': product.get('type'), 'variants': []}
        for variant in product.get('variants', []):
            variant_info = {'id': variant.get('id'), 'price': variant.get('price'), 'name': variant.get('name'), 'public_title': variant.get('public_title'), 'sku': variant.get('sku')}
            product_info['variants'].append(variant_info)
        clothing_sections.append(product_info)
    return clothing_sections

        let filterWrapper;
        let filters = [];
        const filterObserver = new MutationObserver((mutations) => {
          for(const mutation of mutations) {
            if(mutation.addedNodes) {
              mutation.addedNodes.forEach(node => {
                if(node.classList?.contains('collection-list-filters') && filterWrapper) {
                  filterWrapper.appendChild(node.firstElementChild);
                } else if (node.classList?.contains('collection-list-filters') && !filterWrapper) {
                  filters.push(node.firstElementChild);
                } else if(node.classList?.contains('filter-wrapper')) {
                  filterWrapper = node;
                  filterWrapper.append(...filters);
                }
              })
            }
          }
        });
        filterObserver.observe(document.documentElement, {
          childList: true,
          subtree: true
        });

Parsing script:
async def parse_clothing_sections(html: str):
    soup = BeautifulSoup(html, 'html.parser')
    clothing_sections = []
    announcement_slider = soup.find(id='AnnouncementSlider')
    if announcement_slider:
        slides = announcement_slider.find_all(class_='announcement-slider__slide')
        for slide in slides:
            link = slide.find('a', class_='announcement-link')
            if link and 'pajamas' in link.get('href', ''):
                clothing_sections.append(link.get_text(strip=True))
    return clothing_sections

async def parse_clothing_sections(html: str):
    soup = BeautifulSoup(html, 'html.parser')
    clothing_sections = []
    nav_items = soup.find_all('li', class_='mobile-nav__item')
    for item in nav_items:
        link = item.find('a', class_='mobile-nav__link')
        if link:
            text = link.get_text(strip=True)
            href = link.get('href')
            if any((keyword in text.lower() for keyword in ['new', 'arrivals', 'collection', 'pajamas', 'shop'])):
                clothing_sections.append({'text': text, 'href': href})
    return clothing_sections

Parsing script:
async def parse_clothing_sections(html: str):
    soup = BeautifulSoup(html, 'html.parser')
    clothing_sections = []
    clothing_button = soup.find('button', string=lambda text: 'Clothing' in text if text else False)
    if clothing_button:
        parent_div = clothing_button.find_parent('div', class_='mobile-nav__child-item')
        if parent_div:
            collapsible_content = parent_div.find_next_sibling('div', class_='mobile-nav__sublist')
            if collapsible_content:
                links = collapsible_content.find_all('a', class_='mobile-nav__link')
                for link in links:
                    clothing_sections.append({'text': link.get_text(strip=True), 'href': link.get('href')})
    return clothing_sections

Parsing script:
async def parse_clothing_sections(html: str):
    soup = BeautifulSoup(html, 'html.parser')
    clothing_keywords = ['accessories', 'jewelry', 'aprons', 'shoes']
    clothing_sections = []
    items = soup.find_all('li', class_='mobile-nav__item')
    for item in items:
        link = item.find('a', class_='mobile-nav__link')
        if link:
            href = link.get('href', '')
            text = link.get_text(strip=True).lower()
            if any((keyword in href or keyword in text for keyword in clothing_keywords)):
                clothing_sections.append({'text': text, 'href': href})
    return clothing_sections

Parsing script:
async def parse_clothing_sections(html: str):
    soup = BeautifulSoup(html, 'html.parser')
    clothing_sections = []
    top_level_sections = soup.find_all('div', class_='mobile-nav__sublist')
    for section in top_level_sections:
        if 'is-open' in section.get('class', []):
            links = section.find_all('a', class_='mobile-nav__link')
            for link in links:
                clothing_sections.append(link.get_text(strip=True))
    return clothing_sections

Parsing script:
async def parse_clothing_sections(html: str):
    soup = BeautifulSoup(html, 'html.parser')
    sections = []
    collapsible_contents = soup.find_all('div', class_='collapsible-content__inner')
    for content in collapsible_contents:
        section = {}
        links = content.find_all('a', class_='mobile-nav__link')
        section['items'] = [{'name': link.get_text(strip=True), 'url': link['href']} for link in links]
        sections.append(section)
    return sections

Parsing script:
async def parse_clothing_sections(html: str):
    soup = BeautifulSoup(html, 'html.parser')
    clothing_sections = []
    collapsible_contents = soup.find_all('div', class_='collapsible-content__inner')
    for content in collapsible_contents:
        items = content.find_all('li', class_='mobile-nav__item')
        for item in items:
            link = item.find('a', class_='mobile-nav__link')
            if link:
                section_name = link.get_text(strip=True)
                section_link = link.get('href')
                clothing_sections.append((section_name, section_link))
    return clothing_sections

Parsing script:
async def parse_clothing_sections(html: str):
    soup = BeautifulSoup(html, 'html.parser')
    clothing_sections = []
    sublist_div = soup.find('div', class_='mobile-nav__sublist collapsible-content collapsible-content--all')
    if sublist_div:
        list_items = sublist_div.find_all('li', class_='mobile-nav__item')
        for item in list_items:
            link = item.find('a', class_='mobile-nav__link')
            if link:
                clothing_sections.append({'name': link.get_text(strip=True), 'url': link['href']})
    return clothing_sections

Parsing script:
async def parse_clothing_sections(html: str):
    soup = BeautifulSoup(html, 'html.parser')
    clothing_sections = []
    nav_items = soup.find_all('li', class_='mobile-nav__item')
    for item in nav_items:
        link = item.find('a', class_='mobile-nav__link')
        if link and 'collections' in link.get('href', ''):
            clothing_sections.append(link.get('href'))
    return clothing_sections

Parsing script:
async def parse_clothing_sections(html: str):
    soup = BeautifulSoup(html, 'html.parser')
    clothing_sections = []
    sublist_items = soup.select('.mobile-nav__sublist > .mobile-nav__item')
    for item in sublist_items:
        link = item.find('a', class_='mobile-nav__link')
        if link:
            text = link.get_text(strip=True)
            href = link.get('href')
            clothing_sections.append({'text': text, 'href': href})
    return clothing_sections

Parsing script:
async def parse_clothing_sections(html: str):
    soup = BeautifulSoup(html, 'html.parser')
    clothing_sections = []
    items = soup.find_all('li', class_='mobile-nav__item')
    clothing_keywords = ['gift shop', 'accessories', 'shoes', 'ties']
    for item in items:
        link = item.find('a', class_='mobile-nav__link')
        if link and any((keyword in link.text.lower() for keyword in clothing_keywords)):
            clothing_sections.append(link.text.strip())
    return clothing_sections

Parsing script:
async def parse_clothing_sections(html: str):
    soup = BeautifulSoup(html, 'html.parser')
    clothing_sections = []
    clothing_keywords = ['accessories', 'hair-accessories', 'earrings', 'necklaces', 'shoes', 'aprons', 'blankets', 'kids-socks']
    links = soup.find_all('a', href=True)
    for link in links:
        href = link['href']
        if any((keyword in href for keyword in clothing_keywords)):
            clothing_sections.append({'text': link.get_text(strip=True), 'href': href})
    return clothing_sections

Parsing script:
async def parse_clothing_sections(html: str):
    soup = BeautifulSoup(html, 'html.parser')
    clothing_sections = []
    collapsible_sections = soup.find_all('div', class_='mobile-nav__sublist collapsible-content collapsible-content--all')
    for section in collapsible_sections:
        links = section.find_all('a', class_='mobile-nav__link')
        for link in links:
            text = link.get_text(strip=True)
            href = link.get('href')
            clothing_sections.append({'text': text, 'href': href})
    return clothing_sections

Parsing script:
async def parse_clothing_sections(html: str):
    soup = BeautifulSoup(html, 'html.parser')
    clothing_sections = []
    dropdowns = soup.find_all('div', class_='site-nav__dropdown megamenu text-left')
    for dropdown in dropdowns:
        grid_items = dropdown.find_all('div', class_='grid__item')
        for item in grid_items:
            top_level = item.find('a', class_='site-nav__dropdown-link--top-level')
            if top_level and 'clothing' in top_level.text.lower():
                section = {'category': top_level.text.strip(), 'links': []}
                links = item.find_all('a', class_='site-nav__dropdown-link')
                for link in links:
                    section['links'].append({'name': link.text.strip(), 'url': link.get('href')})
                clothing_sections.append(section)
    return clothing_sections

Parsing script:
async def parse_clothing_sections(html: str):
    soup = BeautifulSoup(html, 'html.parser')
    clothing_sections = []
    grid_items = soup.find_all('div', class_='grid__item')
    for item in grid_items:
        section = {}
        title_tag = item.find('div', class_='h5')
        if title_tag and title_tag.a:
            section_title = title_tag.a.get_text(strip=True)
            section['title'] = section_title
        links = []
        link_tags = item.find_all('a', class_='site-nav__dropdown-link')
        for link_tag in link_tags:
            link_text = link_tag.get_text(strip=True)
            link_href = link_tag.get('href')
            links.append({'text': link_text, 'href': link_href})
        section['links'] = links
        clothing_sections.append(section)
    return clothing_sections

Parsing script:
async def parse_clothing_sections(html: str):
    soup = BeautifulSoup(html, 'html.parser')
    clothing_sections = {}
    grid_items = soup.find_all('div', class_='grid__item')
    for item in grid_items:
        top_level_link = item.find('a', class_='site-nav__dropdown-link--top-level')
        if top_level_link:
            category_name = top_level_link.get_text(strip=True)
            clothing_sections[category_name] = []
            sub_links = item.find_all('a', class_='site-nav__dropdown-link')
            for link in sub_links:
                if link != top_level_link:
                    sub_category_name = link.get_text(strip=True)
                    sub_category_href = link.get('href')
                    clothing_sections[category_name].append({'name': sub_category_name, 'href': sub_category_href})
    return clothing_sections

Parsing script:
async def parse_clothing_sections(html: str):
    soup = BeautifulSoup(html, 'html.parser')
    clothing_sections = []
    dropdowns = soup.find_all('div', class_='site-nav__dropdown megamenu text-left')
    for dropdown in dropdowns:
        grid_items = dropdown.find_all('div', class_='grid__item')
        for item in grid_items:
            top_level_link = item.find('a', class_='site-nav__dropdown-link--top-level')
            if top_level_link and top_level_link.text.strip().lower() in ['shop', 'occasion', 'featured']:
                section = {'section_title': top_level_link.text.strip(), 'links': []}
                links = item.find_all('a', class_='site-nav__dropdown-link')
                for link in links:
                    section['links'].append({'text': link.text.strip(), 'href': link.get('href')})
                clothing_sections.append(section)
    return clothing_sections

<script>
  document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", () => {
    document.querySelectorAll('.search-close__button').forEach(btn => {
      btn.addEventListener('click', () => {
        btn.closest('details').removeAttribute('open');
      })
    });
    document.querySelectorAll('.header__search > details').forEach(search => {
      search.addEventListener('toggle', () => {
        search.querySelector('input.field__input').focus();
      })
    });
    
    const siteHeader = document.querySelector('#SiteHeader')
    document.querySelectorAll('.mobile-visible .header__search details').forEach((details) => {
      details.addEventListener('toggle', () => {
        if(details.open) {
          document.body.style.overflow = 'hidden'
        } else {
          document.body.style.overflow = 'auto'
        }
        if(details.open && siteHeader.classList.contains('site-header--stuck')) {
          window.scrollTo({top: 0})
          siteHeader.classList.remove('site-header--stuck');
        }
        if(window.scrollY > 200 && !details.open) {
          siteHeader.classList.add('site-header--stuck');
        }
      })
    })
  })
</script>
<script>
  document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => {
    function closeSearchDrawer() {
      document.removeEventListener('scroll', closeSearchDrawer);
      document.querySelector('.desktop-visible .header__search > details').removeAttribute("open");
    }
    document.querySelector(".desktop-visible .header__search > details").addEventListener('toggle', (ev) => {

    })
  })
</script>
Parsing script:
async def parse_clothing_sections(html: str):
    soup = BeautifulSoup(html, 'html.parser')
    clothing_sections = []
    grid_items = soup.find_all('div', class_='grid__item')
    for item in grid_items:
        section = {}
        top_level = item.find('a', class_='site-nav__dropdown-link--top-level')
        if top_level:
            section['category'] = top_level.get_text(strip=True)
        sub_links = item.find_all('a', class_='site-nav__dropdown-link')
        section['subcategories'] = []
        for link in sub_links:
            href = link.get('href')
            text = link.get_text(strip=True)
            if href and text:
                section['subcategories'].append({'name': text, 'link': href})
        if section:
            clothing_sections.append(section)
    return clothing_sections

<script>
  function sortByChangeHandler(e) {
    const value = e.target.value;
    currentUrl.searchParams.set('sort_by', value);
    window.location = currentUrl.toString();
  }
</script>

async def parse_clothing_sections(html: str):
    soup = BeautifulSoup(html, 'html.parser')
    clothing_sections = []
    sections = soup.find_all('div', class_='shopify-section')
    for section in sections:
        if 'collection' in section.get('id', '') or 'product' in section.get('id', ''):
            clothing_sections.append(section)
    return clothing_sections

Parsing script:
async def parse_clothing_sections(html: str):
    soup = BeautifulSoup(html, 'html.parser')
    clothing_sections = []
    list_items = soup.find_all('li', class_='list-menu__item')
    for item in list_items:
        label = item.find('label', class_='mobile-facets__label')
        if label:
            input_element = label.find('input', type='checkbox')
            if input_element:
                value = input_element.get('value')
                clothing_sections.append(value)
    return clothing_sections

async def parse_clothing_sections(html: str):
    soup = BeautifulSoup(html, 'html.parser')
    clothing_sections = []
    list_items = soup.find_all('li', class_='list-menu__item')
    for item in list_items:
        label = item.find('label')
        if label:
            text = label.get_text(strip=True)
            clothing_sections.append(text)
    return clothing_sections

Parsing script:
async def parse_clothing_sections(html: str):
    soup = BeautifulSoup(html, 'html.parser')
    clothing_sections = []
    list_items = soup.find_all('li', class_='list-menu__item')
    for item in list_items:
        label = item.find('label', class_='mobile-facets__label')
        if label:
            input_element = label.find('input', type='checkbox')
            if input_element:
                size_value = input_element.get('value', '')
                clothing_sections.append(size_value)
    return clothing_sections

async def parse_clothing_sections(html: str):
    soup = BeautifulSoup(html, 'html.parser')
    clothing_sections = []
    list_items = soup.find_all('li', class_='list-menu__item')
    for item in list_items:
        label = item.find('label', class_='mobile-facets__label')
        if label:
            input_element = label.find('input', {'name': 'filter.v.option.size'})
            if input_element:
                size_value = input_element.get('value')
                clothing_sections.append(size_value)
    return clothing_sections

Parsing script:
async def parse_clothing_sections(html: str):
    soup = BeautifulSoup(html, 'html.parser')
    clothing_sections = []
    list_items = soup.find_all('li', class_='list-menu__item')
    for item in list_items:
        label = item.find('label', class_='mobile-facets__label')
        if label:
            input_element = label.find('input', type='checkbox')
            if input_element:
                size_value = input_element.get('value', '')
                clothing_sections.append(size_value)
    return clothing_sections

Parsing script:
async def parse_clothing_sections(html: str):
    soup = BeautifulSoup(html, 'html.parser')
    clothing_sections = []
    list_items = soup.find_all('li', class_='list-menu__item')
    for item in list_items:
        label = item.find('label', class_='mobile-facets__label')
        if label:
            size = label.find('span', aria_hidden='true')
            if size:
                clothing_sections.append(size.text.strip())
    return clothing_sections

Parsing script:
async def parse_clothing_sections(html: str):
    soup = BeautifulSoup(html, 'html.parser')
    clothing_sections = []
    list_items = soup.find_all('li', class_='list-menu__item')
    for item in list_items:
        label = item.find('label')
        if label:
            spans = label.find_all('span', class_=lambda x: x in ['visually-hidden', None])
            clothing_text = ' '.join((span.get_text(strip=True) for span in spans))
            clothing_sections.append(clothing_text)
    return clothing_sections
